### 各文件改动详情

#### 1. `types.ts`

```typescript
export interface ImageItem {
    // ... existing fields ...
    sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic'  // 新增
}
```

#### 2. `constants.ts`

```typescript
export const DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS = [
    { id: 'bing_1920',     name: '必应每日壁纸',          url: 'https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php' },
    { id: 'imgapi_scenic', name: '随机风景 (imgapi.cn)',  url: 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images' },
    { id: 'unsplash_rand', name: 'Unsplash 随机',         url: 'https://source.unsplash.com/random/1920x1080' },
]

export const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL = DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[1]
  // plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg

export function isDynamicUrl(url: string): boolean {
    const clean = url.split('?')[0]
    const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
    return !IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) && !VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) && url.startsWith('http')
}
```

#### 3. `bgRender.ts` — 两个关键改动

```typescript
// ① 接受可选类型强制
export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
    const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
    if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
    else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
}

// ② CSS 双层 background 自动 fallback
export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    if (videoEl) {
        videoEl.style.display = 'none'
        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
    }
    currentMode = 'image'
    canvasEl.style.display = ''
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'
}
```

#### 4. `sourceManager.ts`

```typescript
export async function scanAll(
    assetDirs: string[] = [],
    localFolders: string[] = [],
    dynamicBgUrls: string[] = [],      // 新增参数
): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
    const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [
        scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),
        scanDynamicUrls(dynamicBgUrls),  // 新增
    ]
    // ...
}

export function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {
    return urls.map(url => {
        const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)
        return {
            name: preset?.name ?? new URL(url).hostname,
            url,
            apiPath: url,
            type: 'image' as const,
            sourceType: 'dynamic' as const,
            sourceLabel: 'dynamic',
        }
    })
}
```

#### 5. `index.ts` — 两个入口适配

```typescript
// randomSelect: 加入 dynamicBgUrls 到扫描池
async randomSelect() {
    const dynamicUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")
    const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicUrls)
    // ...
    if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {
        const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
    } else if (item.type === 'image') {
        renderImage(item.url)
    } else {
        renderVideo(item.url)
    }
}

// applyBackground: 处理无后缀的 dynamic URL
private applyBackground() {
    const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
    if (!currentFile) return

    if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {
        const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
    } else if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
        renderVideo(currentFile)
    } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
        renderImage(currentFile)
    } else {
        console.warn(...)
        return
    }
    // ... opacity, blur, position ...
}
```

#### 6. `SourcesTab.svelte` — 顶部新增动态 URL group

```
▼ ☁️ 动态网络壁纸                                          [+添加]
   ├─ [✓] 必应每日壁纸 (https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php)         ← 预设, 无删除
   ├─ [ ] 随机风景 (imgapi.cn)                                        ← 预设
   ├─ [ ] Unsplash 随机                                             ← 预设
   ├─ [✓] https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images    [🗑]    ← 自定义, 可删
   └─ [✓] https://example.com/myapi.php                     [🗑]    ← 自定义, 可删
```

**预设勾选逻辑**：勾选 → 将 URL 加入 `config.dynamicBgUrls`；取消 → 移除。立即 `configStore.save()`。

**自定义 URL 删除**：从 `config.dynamicBgUrls` splice，`configStore.save()`。如果该 URL 是当前背景，触发 `reselectBackground()`。

**`[+添加]` 按钮**：调用新增的 `showAddDynamicUrlDialog(onSuccess(url, isDynamic))`。

#### 7. UrlDialog 扩展（或新 Dialog）— 双模式 URL 输入

```
┌─ 添加网络背景资源 ────────────────────────────┐
│                                                │
│  输入图片 API 或文件 URL                        │
│  [https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing...   ] │
│                                                │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │           🔄 检测中…                      │  │
│  │     或    [预览图]                        │  │
│  │     或    ⚠ URL 后缀不在支持的格式列表中   │  │
│  │     或    ⚠ 网络请求失败                  │  │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                │
│  检测结果: 🌐 动态图像源 (每次返回不同图片)     │
│                              [添加到订阅源]     │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**自动类型判断逻辑**（`checkExt()` 扩展）：

| URL 后缀 | 判定 | 按钮文案 |
|----------|------|---------|
| `.jpg`, `.png`, `.webp` ... | 普通图片 | `上传到缓存` |
| `.mp4`, `.webm` ... | 普通视频 | `上传到缓存` |
| `.php`, 无后缀 ... | **动态源** | `添加到订阅源` |

#### 8. `ConfigTab.svelte` — 当前背景显示

```typescript
function formatCurrentFile(url: string | null): string {
    if (!url) return i18n.none
    if (!isDynamicUrl(url)) return url
    const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)
    if (preset) return `🌐 ${preset.name}`
    const u = new URL(url)
    return `🌐 ${u.hostname}...`
}
```

```svelte
<code class="fn__code">{formatCurrentFile(currentFile)}</code>
```

#### 10. i18n 新增键（12个）

| 键 | 中文 | 用途 |
|----|------|------|
| `dynamicBgGroup` | 动态网络壁纸 | 新 group 标题 |
| `addDynamicUrl` | 添加订阅源 | [+添加] 按钮 |
| `addDynamicUrlTitle` | 添加动态背景源 | Dialog 标题 |
| `detectedDynamic` | 🌐 动态图像源（每次返回不同图片） | 检测结果 |
| `detectedUpload` | 📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地） | 检测结果 |
| `addToDynamic` | 添加到订阅源 | 按钮 (dynamic 模式) |
| `uploadToCache` | 上传到缓存 | 按钮 (upload 模式) |
| `dynamicUrlHint` | 输入图片 API 地址（每次返回不同图片） | 输入框 placeholder |
| `videoBgRecommend` | 视频背景素材推荐 | About 标题 |
| `videoBgRecommendDesc` | 动态订阅源仅支持图片… | About 说明 |
| `presetPrefix` | [预设] | 预设项前缀 |
| `refreshDynamicList` | 刷新订阅源列表 | tooltip |

```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/.agents/plans/20260519_dynamic-bg-url.md",
  "content": "# 动态订阅源功能实施计划\n\n> 创建于 2026-05-19 | 方案 A：直接 canvas URL + CSS 双层 fallback\n\n## 背景\n\n支持类似 `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` 的随机图片 API，每次返回不同背景图。\n\n## 设计决策\n\n| 决策 | 理由 |\n|------|------|\n| **跳过可达性检测** | 失败时 CSS fallback 自动兜底，无需预检+缓存基础设施 |\n| **直接插入 canvas CSS** | `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url(...)` 而非下载到本地 |\n| **CSS 双层 background-image 做 fallback** | `url(dynamic), url(fallback)` — dynamic 失败自动暴露 fallback |\n| **缓存破坏** | 渲染时追加 `?_t=timestamp` |\n| **动态 URL 默认 image 类型** | 不存在返回视频的动态 API |\n| **混合预设+自定义** | 插件内置维护低频失效的预设，用户可添加自己的 URL |\n\n## UI 布局\n\n动态 URL group 放在 SourcesTab **最顶部**：\n\n```\n┌─ 数据源管理 ────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                                                              │\n│  [+ 链接本地目录]  [+ 链接资源目录]                            │\n│                                                              │\n│  ▼ ☁️ 动态网络壁纸                                    [+添加]  │\n│     ├─ [✓] 必应每日壁纸 (https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php) │ ← 预设，无删除\n│     ├─ [ ] 随机风景 (imgapi.cn)                                │ ← 预设\n│     ├─ [ ] Unsplash 随机                                     │ ← 预设\n│     ├─ [✓] https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...            [🗑]      │ ← 自定义，可删\n│     └─ [✓] https://example.com/myapi.php           [🗑]      │ ← 自定义，可删\n│                                                              │\n│  ▼ 📦 Plugin Cache（云同步）              (Images:2 Videos:1) │\n│     ...                                                      │\n│  ▼ 📁 assets/...                                             │\n│     ...                                                      │\n```\n\n\n## 文件改动清单\n\n| # | 文件 | 操作 | 说明 |\n|---|------|------|------|\n| 1 | `src/types.ts` | 修改 | `sourceType` 联合添加 `'dynamic'` |\n| 2 | `src/constants.ts` | 修改 | `DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS` + `DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL` + `isDynamicUrl()` |\n| 3 | `src/stores/config.ts` | 修改 | `AppConfig` 新增 `dynamicBgUrls: string[]` |\n| 4 | `src/services/bgRender.ts` | 修改 | `render(forceType?)` + `renderDynamic(url, fallback)` |\n| 5 | `src/services/sourceManager.ts` | 修改 | `scanDynamicUrls()` + `scanAll` 含 dynamic + `getSourceLabel` |\n| 6 | `src/index.ts` | 修改 | `randomSelect` / `applyBackground` 处理 dynamic 分支 |\n| 7 | `src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte` | 修改 | 顶部新增动态 URL group（预设 checkbox + [+添加] + 自定义删除） |\n| 8 | `src/ui/settings/ConfigTab.svelte` | 修改 | `currentFile` 对 dynamic URL 格式化显示（预设名/域名截断） |\n| 9 | `src/ui/settings/AboutTab.svelte` | 修改 | 视频背景素材站推荐 |\n| 10 | `src/ui/dialogs/index.ts` | 修改 | 新增 `showAddDynamicUrlDialog()` |\n| 11 | `public/i18n/zh_CN.json` | 修改 | ~12 新键 |\n| 12 | `public/i18n/en_US.json` | 修改 | ~12 新键 |\n\n\n## 详细设计\n\n### 1. `src/types.ts`\n\n```typescript\nexport interface ImageItem {\n    name: string\n    url: string\n    apiPath: string\n    type: 'image' | 'video'\n    sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic'  // 新增 'dynamic'\n    sourceLabel: string\n}\n```\n\n### 2. `src/constants.ts`\n\n```typescript\nexport const DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS: { id: string; name: string; url: string }[] = [\n    { id: 'bing_1920',     name: '必应每日壁纸',          url: 'https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php' },\n    { id: 'imgapi_scenic', name: '随机风景 (imgapi.cn)',  url: 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images' },\n    { id: 'unsplash_rand', name: 'Unsplash 随机',         url: 'https://source.unsplash.com/random/1920x1080' },\n]\n\nexport const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL = DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[1]\n// plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg\n\n/**\n * 判断 URL 是否为动态源（无已知图片/视频后缀且是 http 开头）\n */\nexport function isDynamicUrl(url: string): boolean {\n    const clean = url.split('?')[0]\n    const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')\n    return !IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) && !VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) && url.startsWith('http')\n}\n```\n\n### 3. `src/stores/config.ts`\n\n```typescript\nconst APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS: AppConfig = {\n    // ...existing...\n    dynamicBgUrls: [],\n}\n```\n\n### 4. `src/services/bgRender.ts`\n\n```typescript\n// ① render() 接受可选类型强制\nexport function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {\n    const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)\n    if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)\n    else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)\n}\n\n// ② CSS 双层 background-image 实现自动 fallback\nexport function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {\n    if (!canvasEl) return\n    if (videoEl) {\n        videoEl.style.display = 'none'\n        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }\n        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')\n    }\n    currentMode = 'image'\n    canvasEl.style.display = ''\n    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`\n    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'\n}\n```\n\n### 5. `src/services/sourceManager.ts`\n\n```typescript\nexport async function scanAll(\n    assetDirs: string[] = [],\n    localFolders: string[] = [],\n    dynamicBgUrls: string[] = [],   // 新增参数\n): Promise<ImageItem[]> {\n    const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [\n        scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),\n        scanDynamicUrls(dynamicBgUrls),   // 新增\n    ]\n    const validAssetDirs = assetDirs.filter(d => d.length > 0)\n        .map(dir => {\n            const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)\n            return `/data/${normalized}`\n        })\n    tasks.push(...validAssetDirs.map(path => scanSource('assets', path + '/')))\n    // ...local folder logic...\n    const batch = await Promise.all(tasks)\n    return batch.flat()\n}\n\nexport function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {\n    return urls.map(url => {\n        const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)\n        return {\n            name: preset?.name ?? new URL(url).hostname,\n            url,\n            apiPath: url,            // 无本地路径，用 URL 本身\n            type: 'image' as const,\n            sourceType: 'dynamic' as const,\n            sourceLabel: 'dynamic',\n        }\n    })\n}\n\n// getSourceLabel 新增 case\nfunction getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic', path: string): string {\n    switch (type) {\n        case 'dynamic':\n            return 'dynamic'\n        // ...existing cases...\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 6. `src/index.ts`\n\n**randomSelect** — 纳入 dynamic URLs 到随机池：\n\n```typescript\nasync randomSelect() {\n    const assetDirs = configStore.get(\"assetDirs\")\n    const localFolders = configStore.get(\"localFolders\")\n    const dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get(\"dynamicBgUrls\")  // 新增\n    const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicBgUrls)\n    if (pool.length === 0) return\n    const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get(\"currentFile\") : null\n    const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)\n    if (!item) return\n\n    configStore.set(\"currentFile\", item.url)\n    configStore.save()\n\n    if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {\n        const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()\n        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)\n    } else if (item.type === 'image') {\n        renderImage(item.url)\n    } else {\n        renderVideo(item.url)\n    }\n    changeOpacity(configStore.get(\"opacity\"))\n    changeBlur(configStore.get(\"blur\"))\n    changePosition(configStore.get(\"positionX\"), configStore.get(\"positionY\"))\n}\n```\n\n**applyBackground** — 处理无后缀的 dynamic URL：\n\n```typescript\nprivate applyBackground() {\n    try {\n        const currentFile = configStore.get(\"currentFile\")\n        if (!currentFile) return\n\n        // 优先判断动态 URL\n        if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {\n            const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()\n            renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)\n        } else {\n            const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')\n            if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {\n                renderVideo(currentFile)\n            } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {\n                renderImage(currentFile)\n            } else {\n                console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension \"${ext}\" for ${currentFile}`)\n                return\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        // opacity, blur, position...\n    }\n    // autoRefresh timer...\n}\n```\n\n**onload** — 初始化扫描包含 dynamic：\n\n```typescript\n// onload 中 scanAll 调用\nconst dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get(\"dynamicBgUrls\")\nconst pool `UrlDialog.svelte` 或新建 `DynamicUrlDialog.svelte`。扩展现有 `showUrlDialog` 为双模式：\n\n```typescript\nimport DynamicUrlDialog from './DynamicUrlDialog.svelte'\n\nexport function |\n|-------------|------|---------|\n| `.jpg`, `.png`, `.webp` ... | 普通图片 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |\n| `.mp4`, `.webm` ... | 普通视频 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |\n| `.php`, 无后缀 ... | **动态源** → dynamic | `🌐 动态图像源（每次返回不同图片）` |\n\n```typescript\nfunction classifyUrlType(ext: string): 'upload' | 'dynamic' {\n    if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) || VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'upload'\n    return 'dynamic'\n}\n```\n\n### 11. i18n 新增键\n\n| 键 | 中文 | 英文 | 用途 |\n|----|------|------|------|\n| `dynamicBgGroup` | 动态网络壁纸 | Dynamic Web Wallpaper | group 标题 |\n| `addDynamicUrl` | 添加订阅源 | Add Feed | For video backgrounds, download from these sites and add via local upload. | About 说明 |\n| `presetPrefix` | [预设] | [Preset] | 预设项名称前缀 |\n| `removeDynamic` | 移除订阅源 | Remove Feed | 删除 tooltip |\n\n\n## 验证清单\n\n- [ ] 勾选预设 → `dynamicBgUrls` 写入 config，`save()`\n- [ ] 取消勾选预设 → 从 `dynamicBgUrls` 移除\n- [ ] 点击 [+添加] → Dialog 弹出，输入 URL → fetch 检测 → 后缀自动分类\n- [ ] 无后缀 URL → 判定为 dynamic，按钮为「添加到订阅源」\n- [ ] 有图片后缀 URL → 判定为 upload，按钮为「上传到缓存」\n- [ ] 有视频后缀 URL → 判定为 upload，按钮为「上传到缓存」\n- [ ] URL 不可达 → 添加按钮禁用，显示错误信息\n- [ ] 自定义 URL 添加成功 → 出现在 dynamic group 列表中\n- [ ] 自定义 URL 删除 → 从 `dynamicBgUrls` 移除，若为当前背景则触发 reselect\n- [ ] `随机抽一张` → dynamic URL 入选随机池，选中后 cache-bust 渲染\n- [ ] 动态 URL 加载成功 → canvas 显示图片\n- [ ] 动态 URL 加载失败 → CSS fallback 自动显示默认背景图\n- [ ] 关闭再打开背景 → `applyBackground()` 正确识别 dynamic URL 并渲染\n- [ ] 启动时 `changeBgOnStart` → dynamic URL 参与随机，正确渲染\n- [ ] ConfigTab 当前背景 → dynamic URL 显示为预设名或截断域名\n- [ ] AboutTab → 显示视频素材站推荐列表\n- [ ] i18n 中英文切换正常\n- [ ] 预设项无删除按钮（仅 checkbox），自定义 URL 有删除按钮\n- [ ] 删除预设的最后一个\"自定义URL\"后，group 仍可见（预设列表存在）\n\n\n## 禁止事项\n\n- ❌ 不做批量可达性检测和本地缓存\n- ❌ 不支持视频动态 URL\n- ❌ 预设 URL 不提供删除按钮\n- ❌ 不硬编码中文文本（全部走 i18n 键）\n- ❌ 不使用 `createObjectURL` 做缩略图预览\n- ❌ 不在 `for...of` 中串行 `await` 扫描\n"

https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images 这种地址，输入会自动跳转  https://i.33xp.cn/__imgapi.cn__/__imgapi.cn__5cc80efda17d7.jpg， 这种情况是否可以正确处理？

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 11:27:05*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is pointing out that some dynamic image APIs don't return the image directly at the given URL, but instead redirect (HTTP 302) to the actual image URL. For example:

- Input: `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images`
- Redirects to: `https://i.33xp.cn/__imgapi.cn__/__imgapi.cn__5cc80efda17d7.jpg`

This raises several questions about how our Plan A (direct canvas URL) would handle this:

1. **CSS `background-image: url(...)`**: When the browser loads a CSS `url()`, it follows redirects automatically. So if we set `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...?_t=12345')`, the browser will follow the 302 redirect and load the redirected image. This should work fine for CSS.

2. **Cache-busting**: The `?_t=timestamp` parameter is appended to the original URL. The redirect target might have its own query parameters or different behavior. But since the browser follows redirects transparently, the cache-busting should still work - the browser treats the original URL (with `_t`) as a new request each time.

3. **detectType / isDynamicUrl**: The original URL `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...` has `.php` extension, which is correctly classified as dynamic. This works fine.

4. **The issue in UrlDialog**: Looking at the current `UrlDialog.svelte`, it does `fetch(trimmed)` which by default follows redirects (`redirect: 'follow'`). So the content-type check would work - it would get the redirected response with `content-type: image/jpeg`.

5. **However**: After `fetch()` follows the redirect, `response.url` changes to the final URL. But we're storing the original URL in config, not the redirected one. This is correct behavior - we want to re-fetch from the original URL each time so we get different images.

So the redirect case should work fine with Plan A. The browser handles redirects transparently for both CSS `url()` and `fetch()`.

But wait, let me think about potential issues:

1. **Mixed content**: If the original URL is HTTPS but redirects to HTTP, the browser might block it. Similarly, if the original is HTTP and the page is HTTPS. This depends on the specific APIs and the user's environment.

2. **Cross-origin redirects**: CSS `background-image` doesn't have CORS restrictions, so this should be fine.

3. **Redirect loops**: Theoretically possible but unlikely with these APIs.

4. **Performance**: Each redirect adds latency. Not a significant issue for background images.

5. **The UrlDialog detection**: When the user enters `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` in the dialog:
   - `checkExt()` strips `?` → gets `.php` → not in IMAGE_EXTS/VIDEO_EXTS
   - In our new dual-mode logic, this would be classified as `dynamic`
   - Then we do `fetch()` to check reachability → follows redirect → gets image response → confirms it's reachable
   - This should work correctly

So the answer is: **yes, redirects are handled correctly by both CSS rendering and the dialog's reachability check, without any special code**.

The only edge case to consider: if the redirect chain is very long or involves authentication, it might fail. But this is rare for public image APIs.

Let me also think about whether there's any issue with the canvas background-image approach specifically for redirect URLs:

- CSS `url()` in `background-image`: Browser follows redirects natively. ✅
- Cache-busting with `?_t=timestamp`: Works because it changes the original request URL. ✅
- Fallback with double-layer: If redirect fails, fallback shows. ✅

I should also consider: what if the redirect goes to a URL that has a known image extension? For example, redirect from `api.php` to `image.jpg`. The browser and CSS handle this fine - the extension of the redirect source doesn't matter, only the final content.

So my answer is: redirects are handled correctly, no code changes needed. The only thing to verify is that the `UrlDialog`'s `doCheck()` function properly follows redirects (it does, by default fetch follows redirects).

Let me present this analysis clearly.

</details>

重定向情况完全可以正确处理，不需要额外代码。

## 分析

### CSS `background-image` 层

```
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images?_t=12345')
                                    │
                                    ▼ 浏览器原生 302 跟随
                  https://i.33xp.cn/__imgapi.cn__/__imgapi.cn__5cc80efda17d7.jpg
                                    │
                                    ▼ 加载成功 → 渲染
                                    ▼ 加载失败 → fallback Layer 2 自动暴露
```

CSS `url()` 由浏览器引擎处理，**302 重定向透明跟随**，不需要任何 JS 介入。

### Dialog 检测层

当前 `UrlDialog.svelte:44` 的 `fetch(trimmed)` 默认 `redirect: 'follow'`：

```typescript
const resp = await fetch(trimmed)     // 自动跟随 302
const contentType = resp.headers.get('content-type')  // → 'image/jpeg'
```

实际拿到的是重定向后的图片响应，`content-type` 检查正常通过。

### 后缀判定

```
checkExt('https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images')
  → 去 ? 后 → 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php'
  → 后缀 → '.php'
  → 不在 IMAGE_EXTS/VIDEO_EXTS → 判定为 dynamic ✅
```

### cache-busting 仍然有效

`?_t=1234567890` 加在原始 URL 上，浏览器对不同的 `_t` 值发起新请求，每次都会走一遍 302 重定向链到不同图片。

---

**结论：重定向是浏览器的内置能力，CSS `url()` 和 `fetch()` 都原生处理，不需要额外代码。**

5: ## 背景
6: 
7: 支持类似 `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` 的随机图片 API，每次返回不同背景图。
8: 
9: ## 设计决策
10: 
11: | 决策 | 理由 |
12: |------|------|
13: | **跳过可达性检测** | 失败时 CSS fallback 自动兜底，无需预检+缓存基础设施 |
14: | **直接插入 canvas CSS** | `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url(...)` 而非下载到本地 |
15: | **CSS 双层 background-image 做 fallback** | `url(dynamic), url(fallback)` — dynamic 失败自动暴露 fallback |
16: | **缓存破坏** | 渲染时追加 `?_t=timestamp` |
17: | **动态 URL 默认 image 类型** | 不存在返回视频的动态 API |
18: | **混合预设+自定义** | 插件内置维护低频失效的预设，用户可添加自己的 URL |

89: export const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL = "plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/404.jpg"
90: 
91: /**
92:  * 判断 URL 是否为动态源（无已知图片/视频后缀且是 http 开头）
93:  */
94: export function isDynamicUrl(url: string): boolean {
95:     const clean = url.split('?')[0]
96:     const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
97:     return !IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) && !VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) && url.startsWith('http')
98: }
99: ```

110: ### 4. `src/services/bgRender.ts`
111: 
112: ```typescript
113: // ① render() 接受可选类型强制
114: export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
115:     const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
116:     if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
117:     else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
118: }
119: 
120: // ② CSS 双层 background-image 实现自动 fallback
121: export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
122:     if (!canvasEl) return
123:     if (videoEl) {
124:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
125:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
126:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
127:     }
128:     currentMode = 'image'
129:     canvasEl.style.display = ''
130:     canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
131:     canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'
132: }
133: ```
134: 
135: ### 5. `src/services/sourceManager.ts`
136: 
137: ```typescript
138: export async function scanAll(
139:     assetDirs: string[] = [],
140:     localFolders: string[] = [],
141:     dynamicBgUrls: string[] = [],   // 新增参数
142: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
143:     const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [
144:         scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),
145:         scanDynamicUrls(dynamicBgUrls),   // 新增
146:     ]
147:     const validAssetDirs = assetDirs.filter(d => d.length > 0)
148:         .map(dir => {
149:             const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)
150:             return `/data/${normalized}`
151:         })
152:     tasks.push(...validAssetDirs.map(path => scanSource('assets', path + '/')))
153:     // ...local folder logic...
154:     const batch = await Promise.all(tasks)
155:     return batch.flat()
156: }
157: 
158: export function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {
159:     return urls.map(url => {
160:         const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)
161:         return {
162:             name: preset?.name ?? new URL(url).hostname,
163:             url,
164:             apiPath: url,            // 无本地路径，用 URL 本身
165:             type: 'image' as const,
166:             sourceType: 'dynamic' as const,
167:             sourceLabel: 'dynamic',
168:         }
169:     })
170: }
171: 
172: // getSourceLabel 新增 case
173: function getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic', path: string): string {
174:     switch (type) {
175:         case 'dynamic':
176:             return 'dynamic'
177:         // ...existing cases...
178:     }
179: }
180: ```
181: 
182: ### 6. `src/index.ts`
183: 
184: **randomSelect** — 纳入 dynamic URLs 到随机池：
185: 
186: ```typescript
187: async randomSelect() {
188:     const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
189:     const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
190:     const dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")  // 新增
191:     const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicBgUrls)
192:     if (pool.length === 0) return
193:     const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
194:     const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
195:     if (!item) return
196: 
197:     configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
198:     configStore.save()
199: 
200:     if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {
201:         const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
202:         renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
203:     } else if (item.type === 'image') {
204:         renderImage(item.url)
205:     } else {
206:         renderVideo(item.url)
207:     }
208:     changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
209:     changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
210:     changePosition(configStore.get("positionX"), configStore.get("positionY"))
211: }
212: ```
213: 
214: **applyBackground** — 处理无后缀的 dynamic URL：
215: 
216: ```typescript
217: private applyBackground() {
218:     try {
219:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
220:         if (!currentFile) return
221: 
222:         // 优先判断动态 URL
223:         if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {
224:             const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
225:             renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
226:         } else {
227:             const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
228:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
229:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
230:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
231:                 renderImage(currentFile)
232:             } else {
233:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
234:                 return
235:             }
236:         }
237:     } finally {
238:         // opacity, blur, position...
239:     }
240:     // autoRefresh timer...
241: }
242: ```
243: 
244: **onload** — 初始化扫描包含 dynamic：
245: 
246: ```typescript
247: // onload 中 scanAll 调用
248: const dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")
249: const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicBgUrls)
250: ```

256: ```svelte

259:     import { renderDynamic } from "../../services/bgRender"
260: 
261:     // 动态订阅源相关状态

263:

265:         if (dynamicUrls.includes(url)) {
266:             dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
267:         } else {
268:             dynamicUrls = [...dynamicUrls, url]
269:         }

273:         refreshAll()

277:         return DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.some(p => p.url === url)
278:     }
279: 
280:     function removeDynamicUrl(url: string) {
281:         dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)

284:         if (url === configStore.get("currentFile")) reselectBackground()

294:                 refreshAll()

440: 
441: **自动类型判断**（`UrlDialog.svelte` 中 `checkExt` 扩展）：
442: 
443: | URL 后缀模式 | 判定 | 结果标签 |
444: |-------------|------|---------|
445: | `.jpg`, `.png`, `.webp` ... | 普通图片 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |
446: | `.mp4`, `.webm` ... | 普通视频 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |
447: | `.php`, 无后缀 ... | **动态源** → dynamic | `🌐 动态图像源（每次返回不同图片）` |
448: 
449: ```typescript
450: function classifyUrlType(ext: string): 'upload' | 'dynamic' {
451:     if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) || VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'upload'
452:     return 'dynamic'
453: }
454: ```

```typescript

    `plugins/${packageName}/default/av71658201.mp4`,
    `plugins/${packageName}/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg`,
]
```

These paths are served by SiYuan at `plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg`. The 404.jpg is in the same directory, so the path `plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/404.jpg` will work.

24: function siyuanApiPost<T = any>(url: string, data?: any): Promise<T> {
25:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
26:         fetchPost(url, data ?? {}, (response: any) => {
27:             if (response.code === 0) {
28:                 resolve(response.data)
29:             } else {
30:                 reject(new Error(response.msg ?? "fetchPost failed"))
31:             }
32:         })
33:     })
34: }
35: 
36: class ConfigStore {
37:     private cfg: AppConfig = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
38:     private dirty = false
39:     private ready = false
40: 
41:     async load(): Promise<void> {
42:         if (this.ready) return
43: 
44:         let stored: any = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
45: 
46:         if (stored === undefined || stored === null) {
47:             try {
48:                 const all = await siyuanApiPost<Record<string, any>>("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
49:                 stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}
50:             } catch {
51:                 stored = {}
52:             }
53:         }
54: 
55:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
56:         devLog("[bgCover] config loaded, keys:", Object.keys(this.cfg))
57:         this.ready = true
58:     }
59: 
60:     async save(): Promise<void> {
61:         if (!this.dirty || !this.ready) return
62:         devLog("[bgCover] config save")
63:         await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", {
64:             key: STORAGE_KEY,
65:             val: this.cfg,
66:         })
67:         this.dirty = false
68:     }

76:         this.dirty = true
77:     }
78: 
79:     async setAndSave<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): Promise<void> {
80:         this.set(key, value)
81:         await this.save()
82:     }
83:

85:         return { ...this.cfg }

117:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
118:             this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
119:             return

128:                 await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/` })

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I need to make sure renderImage also resets backgroundSize when switching from dynamic back to regular image. The current renderImage sets `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('${url}')` but doesn't set backgroundSize. However, renderDynamic sets `backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'`. When switching from dynamic to regular, we need to reset backgroundSize to 'cover'.

Let me check the current renderImage code... It sets backgroundImage but doesn't touch backgroundSize. The initial `createBgLayer()` sets `backgroundSize = 'cover'` once. So when switching:
1. Start → renderImage(path/to/file.jpg) → backgroundImage updated, backgroundSize stays 'cover' (from createBgLayer) ✅
2. renderDynamic(url, fallback) → sets backgroundSize to 'cover, cover' 
3. Switch back to renderImage → backgroundImage updated to single url, but backgroundSize stays 'cover, cover' ❌

I need to fix renderImage to also reset backgroundSize.

</details>

`renderImage()` 需要恢复 `backgroundSize` 为单层 `cover`，否则从 dynamic 切换回来时会有残余的 `cover, cover`。

'')\n        return IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) || VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) ? ''\n            if (contentType.startsWith('image/')) {\n                if (urlType === 'upload') {\n                    const blob = await resp.blob()\n                    if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)\n                    blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)\n                    previewSrc = blobUrl\n                    validExt = true\n                } else {\n                    isDynamic = true\n                    const blob = await resp.blob()\n                    if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)\n                    blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)\n                    previewSrc = blobUrl\n                }\n            } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {\n                if (urlType === 'upload') {\n                    validExt = true\n                } else {\n                    errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo\n                }\n            } else {\n                errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo\n            }\n        } catch {\n            errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed\n        }\n        checking = false\n    }\n\n    function handleInput() {\n        const trimmed = url.trim()\n        if (!trimmed) {\n            validExt = false\n            isDynamic = false\n            errorMsg = \"\"\n            previewSrc = null\n            return\n        }\n        if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)\n        debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)\n    }\n\n    async function handleUpload() {\n        const trimmed = url.trim()\n        if (!trimmed || !validExt) return\n\n        const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'\n        const destPath = `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`\n\n        const ok = await downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)\n        if (ok) {\n            const renderingUrl = getFileUrl(`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`, 'upload')\n            onSuccess?.(renderingUrl)\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleDynamicAdd() {\n        const trimmed = url.trim()\n        if (!trimmed || !isDynamic) return\n        onDynamicAdd?.(trimmed)\n    }\n\n    function getFileName(): string {\n        return url.trim().split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? ''\n    }\n\n    function canConfirm(): boolean {\n        return validExt || isDynamic\n    }\n\n    onDestroy(() => {\n        if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)\n    })\n</script>"

4. Another possibility: the site might have HTTP redirects or require specific headers. CSS `background-image` doesn't handle redirects the same way as browser navigation.

5. Or it could be that the response is something like a redirect that doesn't work well in CSS background-image context (e.g., the server returns a non-image content-type, or something else).

6. Wait - another possibility: the response might be JSON or HTML that redirects to an image URL, which CSS url() can't follow. Some random image APIs return a redirect or an HTML page that loads the image.

1. CORS/CSP blocking in the Electron webview
2. The server returns a redirect that CSS can't follow
3. Mixed content (HTTP vs HTTPS)
4. The server blocks referrer-based loading
5. The response is not actually a direct image

```html
<canvas id="bglayer" style="background-image: url("https://img.xjh.me/random_img.php?_t=1779157053361"), url("plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/404.jpg"); background-size: cover, cover; ...">
```

Wait - there's a potential issue with the quotes! The style attribute uses `"` for the attribute value, and inside `url()`, the URL is also quoted with `"`. This creates a parsing issue:

```
style="background-image: url("https://..."), url("plugins/..."); ..."
                              ^            ^
```

The browser parser sees: style attribute starts with `"`, then `url(` then `"` which closes the style attribute. The rest is garbage.

But actually, the user's output shows `&quot;` which is the HTML-encoded form. So the DOM inspector shows `url(&quot;...&quot;)`. This is likely just the inspector display format. The actual DOM style property set by JavaScript doesn't have this issue since `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage` is set directly (not via HTML attribute).

是否有可能解析到这类返回html页面中的<img>标签中的src?

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 11:27:05*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is asking if it's possible to parse HTML pages returned by some of these URLs and extract the `<img>` tag's `src` attribute to use as the actual background image.

Let me think about this:

1. `img.xjh.me/random_img.php` returns HTML with `<img alt="..." src="//img.xjh.me/img/63190664_p0.jpg">`
2. `acg.sx/images` returns an HTML gallery page

Could we fetch the HTML, parse it, extract the `<img>` src, and then use THAT URL as the background?

Technically, yes:
1. `fetch(url)` → get HTML
2. Parse with DOMParser → extract `img[src]`
3. Use the extracted src URL as the dynamic background URL

But there are complications:

1. **Different HTML structures**: Each site has different HTML. `img.xjh.me` has a bare `<img>` tag. `acg.sx` has a complex gallery page with multiple images. We'd need site-specific parsers.

2. **Relative URLs**: The `src` might be `//img.xjh.me/img/63190664_p0.jpg` (protocol-relative), `/img/foo.jpg` (root-relative), or `../img/foo.jpg` (relative). We'd need to resolve them against the base URL.

3. **Fragility**: If the site changes its HTML structure, the parser breaks silently.

4. **Performance**: Extra fetch + parse step per background change.

5. **CORS**: The fetch for the HTML page should work (since these are open APIs), but then we'd use a different URL for the actual image in CSS background-image.

The approach would be:
1. For presets that are known to return HTML, add a `parser: 'html-img'` or similar config
2. `fetch()` the URL
3. `new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html')`
4. Query `document.querySelector('img')` or a site-specific selector
5. Extract `src`, resolve it to absolute URL
6. Use that URL (with cache-busting) as the CSS background-image

This is getting complex. A simpler approach might be:
- Just remove HTML-returning URLs from presets (which we already did)
- If the user really wants img.xjh.me, they can find the actual image URL pattern directly

But the user is asking about a more general solution. Let me think about this...

Actually, for these specific sites:
- `img.xjh.me/random_img.php` → returns a single `<img>` tag pointing to a random image
- The actual image pattern seems to be `//img.xjh.me/img/{random_id}.jpg`

For `acg.sx` - this is a full website, not just a random image API. This shouldn't be supported.

For the general case, we could add a `urlType` field to presets:
```typescript
{ id: '...', name: '...', url: '...', type: 'direct' | 'html-img' }
```

But this adds complexity. Let me think about whether it's worth it.

Actually, a simpler approach: we could try to fetch the URL and detect if it returns HTML. If so, try to extract an `<img>` tag and use its `src`. This would work generically without site-specific config.

```typescript
async function resolveImageUrl(url: string): Promise<string | null> {
    const resp = await fetch(url)
    const ct = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
    if (ct.startsWith('image/')) return url // already an image
    
    if (ct.includes('html')) {
        const html = await resp.text()
        const doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html')
        const img = doc.querySelector('img')
        if (img) {
            const src = img.getAttribute('src')
            if (src) return new URL(src, url).href
        }
    }
    return null
}
```

But wait - this changes the architecture. Currently, for dynamic URLs, we set the CSS background-image directly. If we need to fetch + parse HTML first, this becomes async and can't be done in the CSS setter.

We'd need to change the flow for these types of URLs:
1. In `randomSelect()`, when picking a dynamic URL
2. Fetch the URL first
3. If it returns image → use directly
4. If it returns HTML → parse, extract img src, use that
5. Then render with the resolved URL

This would work but adds latency to the background change (a network round-trip before rendering).

Also, we'd need to distinguish between direct-image URLs and HTML-returning URLs in the preset config, or do auto-detection.

**My recommendation:**

For presets, just use URLs that return actual images. Sites that return HTML wrappers aren't suitable for CSS background-image. We already removed the broken ones.

If the user specifically wants `img.xjh.me`, we could:
1. Add it back with a `resolveHtml` flag
2. In the render flow, fetch the HTML, extract the img src, use the resolved URL

But this adds significant complexity for one site that's already somewhat unreliable. The 4 remaining presets all work directly.

Actually, let me think about an even simpler approach: just use a `<img>` element for dynamic URLs instead of CSS background-image. An `<img>` element has `onerror` and we could handle HTML parsing in a pre-fetch step.

Wait no, the whole point of the canvas approach is for CSS styling (cover, position, blur, etc.). Using an `<img>` element would need different styling.

Let me just present the analysis to the user:
- Technically possible but adds complexity
- Each site has different HTML structure (fragile)
- Adds latency (extra network round-trip)
- Better to just use URLs that return direct images
- If a specific HTML-wrapper site is important, we could add site-specific resolvers as a separate feature

I should present this concisely.

</details>

技术上可行，但不推荐。

## 可行性分析

```typescript
// 通用方案：fetch → DOMParser → 提取 img src → 用提取的 URL 渲染
async function resolveImgFromHtml(pageUrl: string): Promise<string | null> {
    const resp = await fetch(pageUrl)
    const ct = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
    if (ct.startsWith('image/')) return pageUrl            // 直接是图
    if (!ct.includes('html')) return null
    const doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(await resp.text(), 'text/html')
    const img = doc.querySelector('img')
    const src = img?.getAttribute('src')
    return src ? new URL(src, pageUrl).href : null         // 解析相对路径
}
```

## 不推荐的原因

| 问题 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| **HTML 结构各异** | `img.xjh.me` 是裸 `<img>`，`acg.sx` 是复杂画廊页，每个站解析规则不同 |
| **脆弱** | 站点改 HTML 结构 → 静默失效，用户不知道原因 |
| **延迟** | 每次切换背景多一次网络往返（fetch HTML → 解析 → 再 fetch 图片） |
| **复杂度** | 需要在 preset 上加 `type: 'html'` 标记，渲染流程分支增加 |
| **收益低** | `img.xjh.me` 等效于 `//img.xjh.me/img/{id}.jpg` 的 wrapper，本质也是静态图 |

## 结论

保留现有策略——预设只收录返回裸图片的 API。HTML wrapper 类型的站点应该找到其底层图片链接模式直接使用，或由用户下载到本地添加。

当前的 4 个预设（必应×2、Unsplash、imgapi）全部返回 `image/jpeg`，无需解析。

19:     let blobUrl = $state<string | null>(null)

25:     function checkExt(u: string): boolean {
26:         const clean = u.split('?')[0]
27:         const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
28:         return VALID_EXTS.has(ext)
29:     }
30: 
31:     async function doCheck(trimmed: string) {
32:         checking = true
33:         errorMsg = ""
34:         validExt = false
35:         previewSrc = null
36: 
37:         if (!checkExt(trimmed)) {
38:             errorMsg = i18n.urlSuffixInvalid
39:             checking = false
40:             return
41:         }
42: 
43:         try {
44:             const resp = await fetch(trimmed)
45:             if (!resp.ok) {
46:                 errorMsg = `${i18n.fetchFailed} (HTTP ${resp.status})`
47:                 checking = false
48:                 return
49:             }
50:             const contentType = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
51:             if (contentType.startsWith('image/')) {
52:                 const blob = await resp.blob()
53:                 if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
54:                 blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
55:                 previewSrc = blobUrl
56:                 validExt = true
57:             } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {
58:                 validExt = true
59:             } else {
60:                 errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo
61:             }
62:         } catch {
63:             errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67:

69:         const trimmed = url.trim()
70:         if (!trimmed) {
71:             validExt = false
72:             errorMsg = ""
73:             previewSrc = null
74:             return
75:         }
76:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
77:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)
78:     }
79: 
80:     async function handleUpload() {
81:         const trimmed = url.trim()
82:         if (!trimmed || !validExt) return
83: 
84:         const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'

1: import { fetchPost } from "siyuan"
2: import { packageName } from "../constants"
3: import { devDebug, devLog } from "../utils/logger"
4: import type { AppConfig } from "../types"
5: 
6: const STORAGE_KEY = packageName
7: 
8: const APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS: AppConfig = {
9:     activate: true,
10:     opacity: 0.5,
11:     blur: 5,
12:     positionX: 50,
13:     positionY: 50,
14:     localFolders: [],
15:     assetDirs: [],
16:     changeBgOnStart: true,
17:     autoRefreshTime: 30,
18:     disabledThemes: { dark: [], light: [] },
19:     imageOverrides: {},
20:     currentFile: null,
21:     inDev: false,
22: }
23: 
24: function siyuanApiPost<T = any>(url: string, data?: any): Promise<T> {
25:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
26:         fetchPost(url, data ?? {}, (response: any) => {
27:             if (response.code === 0) {
28:                 resolve(response.data)
29:             } else {
30:                 reject(new Error(response.msg ?? "fetchPost failed"))
31:             }
32:         })
33:     })
34: }
35: 
36: class ConfigStore {
37:     private cfg: AppConfig = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
38:     private dirty = false
39:     private ready = false
40: 
41:     async load(): Promise<void> {
42:         if (this.ready) return
43: 
44:         let stored: any = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
45: 
46:         if (stored === undefined || stored === null) {
47:             try {
48:                 const all = await siyuanApiPost<Record<string, any>>("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
49:                 stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}
50:             } catch {
51:                 stored = {}
52:             }
53:         }
54: 
55:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
56:         devLog("[bgCover] config loaded, keys:", Object.keys(this.cfg))
57:         this.ready = true
58:     }
59: 
60:     async save(): Promise<void> {
61:         if (!this.dirty || !this.ready) return
62:         devLog("[bgCover] config save")
63:         await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", {
64:             key: STORAGE_KEY,
65:             val: this.cfg,
66:         })
67:         this.dirty = false
68:     }
69: 
70:     get<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K): AppConfig[K] {
71:         return this.cfg[key]
72:     }
73: 
74:     set<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): void {
75:         this.cfg[key] = value
76:         this.dirty = true
77:     }
78: 
79:     async setAndSave<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): Promise<void> {
80:         this.set(key, value)
81:         await this.save()
82:     }
83: 
84:     snapshot(): Readonly<AppConfig> {
85:         return { ...this.cfg }
86:     }
87: 
88:     isLocalPath(path: string): boolean {
89:         return this.cfg.localFolders.some(f => path.startsWith(f))
90:     }
91: 
92:     async reset(): Promise<void> {
93:         console.log("[bgCover] config reset to defaults")
94:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
95:         this.dirty = true
96:         await this.save()
97: 
98:         try {
99:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", {
100:                 keys: [STORAGE_KEY],
101:             })
102:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
103: 
104:         try {
105:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", {
106:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/configs.json`,
107:             })
108:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
109: 
110:         await this.cleanPublicDir()
111:     }
112: 
113:     async cleanOldConfigIfNeeded(): Promise<void> {
114:         const stored = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
115:         if (stored?.crtBgObj !== undefined || stored?.bgObjCfg !== undefined) {
116:             console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版配置 (siyuan.storage)，自动重置为默认")
117:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
118:             this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
119:             return
120:         }
121: 
122:         try {
123:             const files = await siyuanApiPost<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
124:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/`
125:             })
126:             if (Array.isArray(files) && files.length > 0) {
127:                 console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版 petal 数据，自动清理")
128:                 await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/` })
129:             }
130:         } catch {
131:             devDebug("[bgCover] cleanOldConfigIfNeeded: petal dir not found")
132:         }
133:     }
134: 
135:     private async cleanPublicDir(): Promise<void> {
136:         try {
137:             const files = await siyuanApiPost<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
138:                 path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/`,
139:             })
140:             if (!Array.isArray(files)) return
141:             for (const file of files) {
142:                 if (file.isDir) continue
143:                 try {
144:                     await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", {
145:                         path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/${file.name}`,
146:                     })
147:                 } catch { /* ignore */ }
148:             }
149:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
150:     }
151:

16:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost(url, data)
17:     return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
18: }
19: 
20: export async function readSiyuanDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
21:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
22:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
23:     return (data as IDirItem[])
24:         .filter(item => !item.isDir)
25:         .map(item => item.name)
26: }

28: export async function fileExistsRemote(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
29:     if (!path) return false
30:     const parentPath = path.substring(0, path.lastIndexOf('/'))
31:     const targetName = path.substring(path.lastIndexOf('/') + 1)
32:     const files = await readSiyuanDir(parentPath)
33:     return files.includes(targetName)
34: }
35: 
36: export async function readDirItems(path: string): Promise<IDirItem[]> {
37:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
38:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
39:     return data as IDirItem[]
40: }
41: 
42: export async function putFile(path: string, file: File | Blob): Promise<boolean> {
43:     const formData = new FormData()
44:     formData.append("path", path)
45:     formData.append("isDir", "false")
46:     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
47:     formData.append("file", file)
48: 
49:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
50:     return res.code === 0
51: }
52: 
53: export async function removeFile(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
54:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path })
55:     return res.code === 0
56: }
57: 
58: export async function downloadUrl(url: string, destPath: string): Promise<boolean> {
59:     try {
60:         const response = await fetch(url)
61:         if (!response.ok) return false
62:         const blob = await response.blob()
63:         return await putFile(destPath, blob)
64:     } catch (err: any) {
65:         devDebug('[bgCover] api.ts downloadUrl 失败:', url, err.message)
66:         return false

16:     if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'video'

129:     const opacity = 0.99 - 0.25 * clamped

1: import { devDebug } from "./logger"

3: function getFsp(): any {

18:

30: export function getFileUrl(apiPath: string, sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'): string {
31:     if (sourceType === 'local') {
32:         return `file://${apiPath.replace(/\\/g, '/')}`
33:     }
34: 
35:     let rel = apiPath
36:     if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
37:     if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)
38:     else if (rel.startsWith('/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
39:     return rel
40: }
41: 
42: export async function fileExistsLocal(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
43:     if (!path || !isDesktop()) return false
44:     const fsp = getFsp()
45:     try {
46:         await fsp.access(path)
47:         return true
48:     } catch {
49:         return false
50:     }
51: }

(End of file - total 51 lines)
</content>

129:         if (active) {
130:             createBgLayer()
131:             this.applyBackground()
132:         } else {

139:         const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
140:         const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
141:         if (pool.length === 0) {
142:             devLog("[bgCover] randomSelect: pool is empty, nothing to pick")
143:             return
144:         }
145:         const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
146:         const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
147:         if (!item) return
148:         devLog("[bgCover] randomSelect: picked", item.name, "from", pool.length, "items")
149:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
150:         configStore.save()
151:         if (item.type === 'image') {
152:             renderImage(item.url)
153:         } else {
154:             renderVideo(item.url)
155:         }
156:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
157:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
158:         changePosition(configStore.get("positionX"), configStore.get("positionY"))

168:                 return
169:             }
170: 
171:             const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
172:             devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: ext =", ext)
173:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
174:                 devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderVideo")
175:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
176:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
177:                 devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderImage")
178:                 renderImage(currentFile)
179:             } else {
180:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
181:                 return
182:             }
183:         } finally {
184:             const opacity = configStore.get("opacity")
185:             const blur = configStore.get("blur")
186:             const px = configStore.get("positionX")
187:             const py = configStore.get("positionY")
188:             devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: changeOpacity =", opacity, "blur =", blur, "pos =", px, py)
189:             changeOpacity(opacity)
190:             changeBlur(blur)
191:             changePosition(px, py)
192:         }
193: 
194:         const interval = configStore.get("autoRefreshTime")
195:         stopAutoRefresh()
196:         if (interval > 0) {
197:             startAutoRefresh(() => this.randomSelect(), interval * 60000)
198:         }
199:     }
200: 
201:     applyThemeShield() {
202:         if (!configStore.get("activate")) return
203:         if (isCurrentThemeDisabled(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))) {
204:             devLog("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme disabled, hiding")
205:             setVisible(false)
206:         } else {
207:             devLog("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme enabled, showing")
208:             createBgLayer()
209:             this.applyBackground()
210:         }
211:     }
212: }

44:         const newGroups: SourceGroup[] = []
45: 
46:         const uploadFiles = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)
47:         newGroups.push({
48:             type: 'upload',
49:             label: i18n.pluginCache,
50:             path: pluginAssetsDir,
51:             removable: false,
52:             files: uploadFiles,
53:             inaccessible: false,
54:             collapsed: false,
55:             configKey: '',
56:         })
57: 
58:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs").filter(Boolean)
59:         const localFolders = isDesktop() ? configStore.get("localFolders").filter(Boolean) : []
60: 
61:         const assetTasks = assetDirs.map(async (dir) => {
62:             const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)
63:             const path = `/data/${normalized}`
64:             const label = normalized.startsWith('assets/') ? normalized.slice('assets/'.length) : normalized
65:             const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
66:             return { type: 'assets' as const, label, path, files, normalized }
67:         })
68: 
69:         const localTasks = localFolders.map(async (dir) => {

71:             return { type: 'local' as const, label: dir, path: dir, files }
72:         })
73: 
74:         const allScanResults = await Promise.all([...assetTasks, ...localTasks])
75: 
76:         for (const r of allScanResults) {
77:             if (r.type === 'assets') {
78:                 newGroups.push({

## URL-based Background Sources: Complete Code Map

### 1. Dialog Component: `UrlDialog.svelte`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/dialogs/UrlDialog.svelte` (141 lines)

**How it works:**

| Step | Lines | Description |
|------|-------|-------------|
| **Input+debounce** | 68-78 | `handleInput()` uses 500ms debounce before calling `doCheck()` |
| **Extension validation** | 25-29 | `checkExt()` strips query string, extracts extension, validates against `IMAGE_EXTS.union(VIDEO_EXTS)` from `constants.ts` |
| **Content-type verification** | 43-64 | `doCheck()` does a real `fetch(url)` → checks `content-type` header: if `image/` → creates a `Blob` + `createObjectURL` for preview; if `video/` → marks valid but shows "no preview" placeholder |
| **Download+store** | 80-92 | `handleUpload()` calls `downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)` from `api.ts`, which fetches the URL, gets a Blob, and uploads it via `putFile()` to `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>` |
| **Rendering URL construction** | 88-89 | After upload, calls `getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')` from `utils/fs.ts` to build the canvas rendering URL (e.g., `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`) |
| **Callback** | 89 | Calls `onSuccess(renderingUrl)` passing the upload-type rendering URL |
| **Alt: Enter key** | 109 | `Enter` key triggers `handleUpload()` directly when `validExt` is true |

**Key dependencies:**
- `downloadUrl()` from `../../utils/api.ts` (line 3)
- `getFileUrl()` from `../../utils/fs.ts` (line 4)
- `IMAGE_EXTS`, `VIDEO_EXTS` from `../../constants` (line 5)

---

### 2. Dialog Factory: `dialogs/index.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/dialogs/index.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 43-57 | `showUrlDialog(onSuccess)` | Wraps `UrlDialog.svelte` in `svelteDialog()`. Passes `onSuccess` prop; when dialog's `handleUpload()` succeeds, it calls `onSuccess(uploadUrl)` then closes the dialog. |

Imported by:
- `topbarMenu.ts` (line 8)
- `SourcesTab.svelte` (line 15)

---

### 3. Config Store: URL Storage
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/stores/config.ts`

**Config schema** (from `src/types.ts`, lines 11-25):

```typescript
export interface AppConfig {
    // ... other fields ...
    currentFile: string | null    // ← stores the rendering URL of the currently active background
    // ...
}
```

**How URLs are stored:**
- There is **NO dedicated "urls" config key**. All URL-sourced backgrounds become `upload`-type files.
- When a URL is downloaded, it's saved to `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>`
- The `currentFile` config key stores the **canvas rendering URL** (e.g., `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`)
- The file exists alongside other upload-type files in the `pluginAssetsDir` (`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/`)

**No separate "urlSources" list exists** -- URL sources are merged into the `upload` source type group.

---

### 4. URL Download: `api.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/utils/api.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 58-68 | `downloadUrl(url, destPath)` | 1. `fetch(url)` the remote resource; 2. `response.blob()` to get binary; 3. `putFile(destPath, blob)` uploads to siyuan's file system. Returns `boolean`. |

**The full download pipeline:**
```
UrlDialog.svelte:handleUpload()
  → api.downloadUrl(url, "data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>")
    → fetch(url) → response.blob()
    → api.putFile(destPath, blob)
      → FormData { path, isDir, modTime, file }
      → fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
  → fs.getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')  # builds rendering URL
  → onSuccess(renderingUrl)            # callback to topbarMenu or SourcesTab
```

---

### 5. URL-to-Rendering-URL Conversion: `fs.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/utils/fs.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 30-40 | `getFileUrl(apiPath, sourceType)` | For `'upload'` type (and `'assets'`): strips `/data/` prefix, resulting in relative webview paths like `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`. For `'local'` type: prepends `file://`. |

**Path transformation for upload:**
```
Input:  /data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg
Output: public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg
```
This relative path is what gets stored in `currentFile` and used in `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/...')`.

---

### 6. Source Scanning: `sourceManager.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/services/sourceManager.ts`

| Lines | Function | URL-related behavior |
|-------|----------|---------------------|
| 10-43 | `scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)` | Always scans `upload` group (line 15: `scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)`). URL-downloaded files are discovered here alongside other upload-type files. |
| 45-83 | `scanSource(type, path)` | For `upload`/`assets`: calls `readSiyuanDir(path)` (siyuan API); For `local`: calls `readLocalDir(path)`. Each file gets its `url` via `getFileUrl(apiPath, type)` at line 66. |
| 85-97 | `pickRandom(items, excludeUrl?)` | Used for random selection; can exclude current URL. |

---

### 7. Background Rendering: `bgRender.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/services/bgRender.ts`

| Lines | Function | URL-related behavior |
|-------|----------|---------------------|
| 13-19 | `detectType(url)` | Determines image vs video from file extension in the URL |
| 66-70 | `render(url)` | Dispatches to `renderImage` or `renderVideo` |
| 72-84 | `renderImage(url)` | Sets `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('${url}')` -- the URL is used directly in CSS |
| 86-102 | `renderVideo(url)` | Sets `videoEl.src = url` |

---

### 8. Call-Sites: Where URL dialogs are invoked

**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/topbarMenu.ts`
- **Lines 97-106**: Topbar menu → "添加网络资源" → calls `showUrlDialog()` → on success: saves `uploadUrl` to `currentFile`, calls `renderImage`/`renderVideo`.

**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte`
- **Lines 277-292**: Settings panel → upload group's link button → calls `showUrlDialog()` → on success: saves to `currentFile`, renders, then `refreshAll()`.
- **Lines 354-359**: The "link" icon button in the upload group header.

---

### 9. Type Definitions
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/types.ts`

| Lines | Type | Fields relevant to URLs |
|-------|------|------------------------|
| 11-25 | `AppConfig` | `currentFile: string \| null` -- stores the rendering URL |
| 27-34 | `ImageItem` | `url: string` (rendering URL), `apiPath: string` (filesystem path), `sourceType: 'local' \| 'upload' \| 'assets'` |

**URL sources always have `sourceType: 'upload'`**, because they are downloaded into the plugin's public directory.

---

### Summary: Current URL Source Lifecycle

```
User enters URL in UrlDialog.svelte
  │
  ├─ Debounced validation (500ms): check file extension + HTTP content-type
  │
  ├─ User clicks "确认"
  │
  ├─ api.downloadUrl(url, destPath)
  │   ├─ fetch(url) → blob
  │   └─ api.putFile(destPath, blob) → saves to data/public/<plugin>/<filename>
  │
  ├─ fs.getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')
  │   └─ Strips /data/ prefix → "public/<plugin>/<filename>"
  │
  ├─ onSuccess(renderingUrl) callback
  │   ├─ configStore.set("currentFile", renderingUrl)
  │   ├─ configStore.save()
  │   └─ bgRender.render(renderingUrl)
  │       └─ canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/<plugin>/<filename>')
  │
  └─ File appears in upload group alongside other upload-type files
```

**Key design decision:** URL sources are **not a separate source type**. They are downloaded once and become permanent `upload`-type files, indistinguishable from files uploaded via the "上传多个文件" or "上传整个目录" options. There is no config key that tracks "URL origin" -- only the rendering URL in `currentFile` and the file in the plugin's public directory.

## 1. `src/stores/config.ts` (159 行)

**配置存储单例类**，负责读取/写入 SiYuan 本地存储中的插件配置。

**默认配置 (`APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS`)：**

| 字段 | 类型 | 默认值 | 说明 |
|------|------|--------|------|
| `activate` | `boolean` | `true` | 是否激活背景 |
| `opacity` | `number` | `0.5` | 透明度 (用户设置域 `[0.1, 1]`，加权后域 `[0.74, 0.99]`) |
| `blur` | `number` | `5` | 模糊度 |
| `positionX` | `number` | `50` | 背景水平位置 (%) |
| `positionY` | `number` | `50` | 背景垂直位置 (%) |
| `localFolders` | `string[]` | `[]` | 本地文件夹绝对路径列表 (desktop only) |
| `assetDirs` | `string[]` | `[]` | 资源目录路径列表 (assets 类型) |
| `changeBgOnStart` | `boolean` | `true` | 启动时自动切换背景 |
| `autoRefreshTime` | `number` | `30` | 自动刷新间隔 (分钟) |
| `disabledThemes` | `DisabledThemes` | `{ dark: [], light: [] }` | 屏蔽的主题 |
| `imageOverrides` | `Record<string, ImageOverride>` | `{}` | 图片级别的覆盖配置 (位置等) |
| `currentFile` | `string \| null` | `null` | 当前背景文件路径 |
| `inDev` | `boolean` | `false` | 开发模式开关 |

**核心方法：**
- `load()` — 从 `window.siyuan.storage` 或 `/api/storage/getLocalStorage` 加载
- `save()` — 脏标记防抖写入 `/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal`
- `get/set/setAndSave` — 类型安全的属性访问
- `snapshot()` — 返回只读快照
- `isLocalPath(path)` — 判断路径是否属于 `localFolders` 列表
- `reset()` — 重置为默认值，清理 petal 旧数据和 public 上传文件
- `cleanOldConfigIfNeeded()` — 自动检测旧版配置并迁移

---

## 2. `src/types.ts` (42 行)

**所有类型定义：**

```typescript
// 主题屏蔽（按暗色/亮色分组）
export interface DisabledThemes {
    dark: string[]
    light: string[]
}

// 单张图片级别的覆盖配置
export interface ImageOverride {
    positionX?: number
    positionY?: number
}

// 根配置对象（与 config.ts 默认值一一对应）
export interface AppConfig {
    activate: boolean
    opacity: number
    blur: number
    positionX: number
    positionY: number
    localFolders: string[]
    assetDirs: string[]
    changeBgOnStart: boolean
    autoRefreshTime: number
    disabledThemes: DisabledThemes
    imageOverrides: Record<string, ImageOverride>
    currentFile: string | null
    inDev: boolean
}

// 背景图片/视频项（渲染引擎使用）
export interface ImageItem {
    name: string          // 文件名 (显示用)
    url: string           // 用于 CSS background-image / video src 的 URL
    apiPath: string       // 思源 API 路径 (用于上传/删除操作)
    type: 'image' | 'video'
    sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
    sourceLabel: string   // 来源标签 (如目录名或 URL 描述)
}

// 源配置（表示一组文件来源）
export interface SourceConfig {
    type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
    path: string
    label: string
}
```

底部从 `constants` 重导出：`IMAGE_EXTS`、`VIDEO_EXTS`、`classifyFileType`。

---

## 3. `src/constants.ts` (42 行)

**全局常量与工具函数：**

```typescript
export const packageName = "siyuan-plugin-background-cover"
export const packageVersion = pluginJson.version   // 从 plugin.json 读取

// 支持的图片扩展名 (Set)
export const IMAGE_EXTS = new Set([
    '.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.jfif', '.gif', '.webp', '.bmp', '.svg', '.avif',
])

// 支持的视频扩展名 (Set)
export const VIDEO_EXTS = new Set([
    '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov', '.avi', '.mkv',
])

// 上传文件存储路径前缀
export const pluginAssetsDir = `/data/public/${packageName}/`

// 默认内置背景文件 (随机抽取)
export const DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS = [
    `plugins/${packageName}/default/av71658201.mp4`,
    `plugins/${packageName}/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg`,
]

export function pickDefaultBackground(): string  // 随机返回默认背景

// 根据文件名后缀分类文件类型
export function classifyFileType(filename: string): 'image' | 'video' | null

// 顶栏 SVG 图标定义
export const pluginTopIcon = { iconLogo: '<symbol>...</symbol>' }
```

---

## 数据结构关系总结

```
AppConfig (持久化到思源 localStorage)
  ├── 全局设置: activate, opacity, blur, positionX, positionY
  ├── 自动行为: changeBgOnStart, autoRefreshTime
  ├── 源列表:   localFolders (string[]), assetDirs (string[])
  ├── 运行时:   currentFile (string|null)
  ├── 高级:     disabledThemes, imageOverrides, inDev
  │
  └── [扫描时生成] ──→ ImageItem[] (不在 AppConfig 中，由 sourceManager 运行时构建)
                        ├── name, url, apiPath
                        ├── type: 'image' | 'video'
                        ├── sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
                        └── sourceLabel

三种源类型 (SourceConfig):
  local   → desktop only, fsp.readdir, url("file:///absolute/path/img.jpg")
  upload  → 全平台, readSiyuanDir, url("public/{packageName}/img.jpg")
  assets  → 全平台, readSiyuanDir, url("assets/.../img.jpg")
```
